#### What this PR does / why we need it:

This PR implements the support for DRA devices in Kueue workloads.




#### Which issue(s) this PR fixes:
<!--
*Automatically closes linked issue when PR is merged.
Usage: `Fixes #<issue number>`, or `Fixes (paste link of issue)`.

Fixes #2941


#### Special notes for your reviewer:

Work Item Checklist for reviewers:
- [x] Add DRAConfig API 
- [x] Add feature gates and API validations
- [x] Implement resource accounting behind a feature gate
   - [x] Accounting for ResourceClaimTemplates
   - [x] Accounting for ResourceClaims
- [x] find alternatives for this: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/5873#discussion_r2223241244
- [x] move the implementation to v1beta2 API
- [x] add basic integration/sanity tests
- [x] move DynamicResourceAllocationConfig CRD to clusterscoped
- [x] remove the CRD in favor of configmap that loads the mapping at controller start
- [x] remove support for resource claims
- [x] move processing of DRA workloads in Reconcile function of DRA instead of event handlers 

Nice to haves:
- [ ] Add integration for config change https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/5873#discussion_r2344377833
- [ ] support for resource claim templates with DeviceAllocationModeAll  https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/5873#discussion_r2344615191
- [ ] Add event+status condition for dra processing failure for UX
- [ ] Check if it will be valuable to assert presence of device classes when dra configuration is loaded in kueue: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/5873#discussion_r2349039588
- [ ] Move the pre-existing logic in workload_controller from event handlers to Reconcile: [https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/5873#issuecomment-3299784921](comment), related issue: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/5310
- [ ] Re-evaluate a need for an extra check in scheduler about existence of ResourceClaimTemplates / ResourceClaims: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/5873#discussion_r2352245285 before entering Beta

Notes:
- [ ] document the side-effects of enabling->disabling->re-enabling this feature
 
#### Does this PR introduce a user-facing change?

### Comment by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2025-08-11T18:59:14Z

Ok, I will continue tomorrow, but it feels supporting the live reloading makes the PR overwhelming for review currently. I would suggest only parse the mapping and pass it into NewInfo. 

We need some prepratory work of propagating Context and Errors to support live reloading properly without cutting corners. This refers to comments like https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/5873#discussion_r2267639711 and https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/5873#discussion_r2267705032

### Comment by [@alaypatel07](https://github.com/alaypatel07) — 2025-08-11T20:00:07Z

Discussed with @mimowo on slack here are the issues with the current implementation:

1. the lookup function from cache into queue is leaking abstractions
2. context needs to be plumbed wherever the resource claim or resource claim template is fetched from k8s api
3. whatever abstraction evaluates the quota needs to send back errors directly

In order to make the code changes in the PR aligned with future direction, it needs to be simplified with the following steps:

1. kueue controller-manager will read mapping when it starts and save it in memory.
2. when a DRA related workload is created, workload_controller.go will fetch the resourceclaim/resource claim templates and     use the in-memory mapping from step one to generate a resource-name -> count for the workload. (context, errors and lookup handled here)
3. workload controller will send the resource-name ->count value to workload.Info when through InfoOptions, queue package will reserve the resources for it and update cluster queue status
4. workload will be admitted/suspended
5. if workload is admitted cache package will calculate usage from cluster queue status, it will not require the workload.Info from DRAInfoOptions because the cluster queue status already has the results from admission
6. if the admin wants to change the mapping, they have to delete all the DRA workloads, update the CRD and restart kueue


cc @tenzen-y @kannon92 for viz

I will work on simplifying the implementation based on the above discussion

### Comment by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2025-08-12T16:21:53Z

Today we also synced with @alaypatel07 and my two comments are:
- I would like to migrate away from webhook to CEL
- about the feature gate strategy. 

First when we add a new controller then it is simple- just gate registering the controller, but don't check the gate inside
Second, when the new code is injected into pre-existing code, then we have two choices:
1. rely on the side effects of enabling the feature gate (like some fields)
2. check the feature gate + rely on the side effects

I belong to the (2.) camp, even it checking the gate feels extra, because (a) the gate will be deleted one day, (b) it makes it really clear if the side effects are iff the gate is enabled, (c) allow to quickly answer the questions like "give me all places modified by the feature" - we can just search by the feature gate occurrences. Otherwise it becomes much more subtle.

### Comment by [@alaypatel07](https://github.com/alaypatel07) — 2025-08-12T16:29:40Z

@mimowo thanks for the summary, I will work on the CEL now that we have alignment on the core resource accounting functionality

### Comment by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2025-09-08T16:31:03Z

@tenzen-y @alaypatel07 I'm also yet thinking we could go with ConfigMap instead of CRD. Seems like the CRD introduces extra complexity. Also, the ConfigMap would be more consistent with what we have until now. 

Finally, using ConfigMap could make it a bit easier to graduate API to v1beta2 for all features consistently. Wdyt?

### Comment by [@alaypatel07](https://github.com/alaypatel07) — 2025-09-08T18:44:27Z

> I'm also yet thinking we could go with ConfigMap instead of CRD. Seems like the CRD introduces extra complexity. Also, the ConfigMap would be more consistent with what we have until now.

> Finally, using ConfigMap could make it a bit easier to graduate API to v1beta2 for all features consistently. Wdyt?

@mimowo I think having CRD allows for use to use CEL and completely remove the webhook from validations. If we bring back the configmap, we will have to re-add the already removed validations to the start of the kueue-controller-manager.

Considering that we now have CEL validations with CRD and have completely removed the validation code, I would prefer to have a CRD unless there are any red flags that were missed with this approach. Curious to hear what others think as well.

cc @kannon92 as well

### Comment by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2025-09-08T19:17:07Z

> @mimowo I think having CRD allows for use to use CEL and completely remove the webhook from validations. If we bring back the configmap, we will have to re-add the already removed validations to the start of the kueue-controller-manager.

I know, but in exchange it should save complexity on the controller. Also, tests probably.

> Considering that we now have CEL validations with CRD and have completely removed the validation code, I would prefer to have a CRD unless there are any red flags that were missed with this approach. Curious to hear what others think as well.

I expect the validation code to be relatively easy to transfer to ConfigMap. 

>  I would prefer to have a CRD unless there are any red flags that were missed with this approach

not sure about clear red flags, but two aspects:
(a) consitency with "multiKueue", "resourceTranformations" or "cert-manager" configurations
(b) amount of code (could drop the controllers)
(c) would leave us without the any Alpha APIs for a time being (after TAS is graduated to beta, hopefully 0.14). So, it would allow us to graduate to v1beta2 all APIs at once in 0.15.

I know some users may want live reloading, but given the complexity of the PR, I'm really reluctant to make it any more complex than bare minimum.

Also input from @tenzen-y and @gabesaba would be great.

### Comment by [@alaypatel07](https://github.com/alaypatel07) — 2025-09-09T13:25:30Z

@mimowo I agree on the simplicity of the configmap solution, it will indeed remove some complexity. But I am concerned that with the alternative approach the complexity is simply to a future release, some day it will have to be solved and I am wondering if it will take more work to solve it in the future then doing it now.

Having said that, I am open to going either way, if reviewers feel the configmap approach is the right way, I will modify this PR accordingly.

### Comment by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2025-09-11T16:56:57Z

### Comment by [@alaypatel07](https://github.com/alaypatel07) — 2025-09-11T17:06:25Z

### Comment by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2025-09-16T17:54:34Z

One general-level remark is that we currently silence errors from event handlers in the workload_controller in a couple of places, this is not good becuase errors in event handlers are not re-tried. We should instead move the logic to the Reconcile function. We've decided with this PR to go in this direction, avoiding repeating the anti-pattern, but it means a bit of inconcistency in how workloads are handled, thus logs like "log.V(2).Info("Skipping queue update for DRA workload - handled in Reconcile")". We already have an open issue that could align this in the long run: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/5310

```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,92 @@

+package core

+import (
+	"context"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"

+)
+
+// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=get;list;watch
+
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler keeps the cache's DeviceClass→logical-resource
+// mapping in sync with the singleton DynamicResourceAllocationConfig object.
+// It is only registered when the DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is enabled.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	cache  *cache.Cache
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+func NewDRAConfigReconciler(client client.Client, c *cache.Cache) *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler {
+	return &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		cache:  c,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName("dra-config-reconciler"),
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+
+	var cfg kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig
+	if err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &cfg); err != nil {
+		// TODO: this should never happen. But if a user deletes the singleton DRA by mistake, we should
+		//  have a way to gracefully handle it. May be adding a finalizer to the singleton DRAConfig object?
+		return ctrl.Result{}, client.IgnoreNotFound(err)
+	}
+
+	r.log.V(2).Info("Reconciling DynamicResourceAllocationConfig", "name", req.NamespacedName)
+	// we do not expect a lot of reconciles triggered here, therefore directly updating the cache should be okay
+	r.cache.AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(r.log, &cfg)
+	return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
```

  No need to check the feature gate inside the reconciler since the controller installation is guarded by the feature gate already.

```diff
+package webhooks

+import (
+	"context"
+
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/validation/field"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/webhook"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/webhook/admission"
```

```diff
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/features"
+)
+
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook validates create / update requests.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook struct{}
+
+func setupWebhookForDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
+	return ctrl.NewWebhookManagedBy(mgr).
+		For(&kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{}).
+		WithValidator(&DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook{}).
+		Complete()
+}
+
+// +kubebuilder:webhook:path=/validate-kueue-x-k8s-io-v1alpha1-dynamicresourceallocationconfig,mutating=false,failurePolicy=fail,sideEffects=None,groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=create;update,versions=v1alpha1,name=vdynamicresourceallocationconfig.kb.io,admissionReviewVersions=v1
+
+var _ webhook.CustomValidator = &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook{}
+
+// ValidateCreate blocks CR creation when the feature-gate is off.
+func (w *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook) ValidateCreate(_ context.Context, obj runtime.Object) (admission.Warnings, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return nil, field.Forbidden(field.NewPath(""), "DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is disabled")
+	}
+	draCfg := obj.(*kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+
+	var allErrs field.ErrorList
+	if draCfg.Name != "default" {
+		allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(field.NewPath("metadata", "name"), draCfg.Name, "must be 'default'"))
+	}
+
+	if draCfg.Namespace != "kueue-system" {
+		allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(field.NewPath("metadata", "namespace"), draCfg.Namespace, "must be 'kueue-system'"))
+	}
+
+	if len(allErrs) > 0 {
+		return nil, allErrs.ToAggregate()
+	}
+
+	// structural validation of spec
+	allErrs = append(allErrs, validateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(draCfg)...)
+	if len(allErrs) > 0 {
+		return nil, allErrs.ToAggregate()
+	}
+	return nil, nil
+}
+
+// ValidateUpdate blocks updates when the feature-gate is off.
+func (w *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook) ValidateUpdate(_ context.Context, _ runtime.Object, newObj runtime.Object) (admission.Warnings, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return nil, field.Forbidden(field.NewPath(""), "DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is disabled")
+	}
+	draCfg := newObj.(*kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+	var allErrs field.ErrorList
+
+	if draCfg.Name != "default" {
```

  You should move this to CEL or kubebuilder validation.
  
  Try and limit what we put in webhook code.

```diff
+					DeviceClassNames: []corev1.ResourceName{dcName},

+func TestValidateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(t *testing.T) {
```

  Playing around with Copilot on reviews.
  
  I see some missing test cases:
  
  Certainly! Here are some additional test cases you could add to the TestValidateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig function to increase coverage and robustness:
  
  ### 1. Empty Resources List
  Test the behavior when the resources list in the config is empty.
  
  ```go
  "empty resources": {
  	cfg: &kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{
  		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
  			Name:      "default",
  			Namespace: "kueue-system",
  		},
  		Spec: kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfigSpec{
  			Resources: []kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResource{},
  		},
  	},
  	wantErr: field.ErrorList{
  		// Expect an error if an empty list is not allowed
  	},
  },
  ```
  
  ### 2. Duplicate Resource Names
  Test for duplicate resource names in the resources array.
  
  ```go
  "duplicate resource names": {
  	cfg: &kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{
  		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
  			Name:      "default",
  			Namespace: "kueue-system",
  		},
  		Spec: kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfigSpec{
  			Resources: []kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResource{
  				{Name: "example.com/gpu", DeviceClassNames: []corev1.ResourceName{"example.com/device-class"}},
  				{Name: "example.com/gpu", DeviceClassNames: []corev1.ResourceName{"example.com/device-class-2"}},
  			},
  		},
  	},
  	wantErr: field.ErrorList{
  		// Expect an error for duplicate resource names
  	},
  },
  ```
  
  ### 3. Nil DeviceClassNames
  Test when DeviceClassNames is nil or empty.
  
  ```go
  "empty deviceClassNames": {
  	cfg: &kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{
  		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
  			Name:      "default",
  			Namespace: "kueue-system",
  		},
  		Spec: kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfigSpec{
  			Resources: []kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResource{
  				{Name: "example.com/gpu", DeviceClassNames: []corev1.ResourceName{}},
  			},
  		},
  	},
  	wantErr: field.ErrorList{
  		// Expect an error if deviceClassNames must not be empty
  	},
  },
  ```
  
  ### 4. Multiple Invalid DeviceClassNames
  Test for multiple invalid device class names in the list.
  
  ```go
  "multiple invalid device class names": {
  	cfg: makeConfig(corev1.ResourceName("example.com/gpu"), corev1.ResourceName("@invalid1")),
  	wantErr: field.ErrorList{
  		field.Invalid(resourcesPath.Index(0).Child("deviceClassNames").Index(0), "@invalid1", ""),
  	},
  },
  ```
  (You could expand this to have multiple device class names, some of which are invalid.)
  
  ### 5. Resource Name is an Empty String
  Test for a resource with an empty string as the name.
  
  ```go
  "empty resource name": {
  	cfg: makeConfig(corev1.ResourceName(""), corev1.ResourceName("example.com/device-class")),
  	wantErr: field.ErrorList{
  		field.Invalid(resourcesPath.Index(0).Child("name"), "", ""),
  	},
  },
  ```
  
  ### 6. Device Class Name is an Empty String
  Test for a device class name that's an empty string.
  
  ```go
  "empty device class name": {
  	cfg: makeConfig(corev1.ResourceName("example.com/gpu"), corev1.ResourceName("")),
  	wantErr: field.ErrorList{
  		field.Invalid(resourcesPath.Index(0).Child("deviceClassNames").Index(0), "", ""),
  	},
  },
  ```
  
  ---
  
  These suggestions assume that your validation logic should catch these cases. If some are already handled, you can adjust or skip as needed. Let me know if you want example code for any of these!

- **pkg/cache/cache.go:1034** by [@tenzen-y](https://github.com/tenzen-y) — 2025-07-18T16:21:52Z
```diff
@@ -986,3 +989,30 @@ func (c *Cache) MatchingClusterQueues(nsLabels map[string]string) sets.Set[kueue
 func queueKey(q *kueue.LocalQueue) queue.LocalQueueReference {
 	return queue.NewLocalQueueReference(q.Namespace, kueue.LocalQueueName(q.Name))
 }
+
+// AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig ingests the singleton CRD and updates
+// the in-memory DeviceClass → logical resource map.
+// It is idempotent and thread-safe.
+func (c *Cache) AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(log logr.Logger, draCfg *kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig) {
+	c.Lock()
+	defer c.Unlock()
+
+	// Rebuild from scratch to avoid stale entries.
+	newMap := make(map[corev1.ResourceName]corev1.ResourceName)
+	for _, res := range draCfg.Spec.Resources {
+		for _, dc := range res.DeviceClassNames {
+			newMap[dc] = res.Name
+		}
+	}
+	c.draDeviceClassToResource = newMap
+	log.V(2).Info("Updated DRA DeviceClass mapping", "entries", len(newMap))
+}
+
+// GetResourceNameForDeviceClass converts a DeviceClass to its logical resource name.
+// Returns (logicalRes, true) on success or ("", false) when unmapped.
+func (c *Cache) GetResourceNameForDeviceClass(dc corev1.ResourceName) (corev1.ResourceName, bool) {
+	c.RLock()
+	defer c.RUnlock()
+	lr, ok := c.draDeviceClassToResource[dc]
+	return lr, ok
```

  ```suggestion
  	return c.draDeviceClassToResource[dc]
  ```
  
  Simplify the implementations.

```diff
+package core
+
+import (
+	"context"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/cache"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/features"
+)
+
+// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=get;list;watch
+
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler keeps the cache's DeviceClass→logical-resource
+// mapping in sync with the singleton DynamicResourceAllocationConfig object.
+// It is only registered when the DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is enabled.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	cache  *cache.Cache
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+func NewDRAConfigReconciler(client client.Client, c *cache.Cache) *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler {
+	return &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		cache:  c,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName("dra-config-reconciler"),
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+
+	var cfg kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig
+	if err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &cfg); err != nil {
+		// TODO: this should never happen. But if a user deletes the singleton DRA by mistake, we should
+		//  have a way to gracefully handle it. May be adding a finalizer to the singleton DRAConfig object?
+		return ctrl.Result{}, client.IgnoreNotFound(err)
+	}
+
+	r.log.V(2).Info("Reconciling DynamicResourceAllocationConfig", "name", req.NamespacedName)
+	// we do not expect a lot of reconciles triggered here, therefore directly updating the cache should be okay
+	r.cache.AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(r.log, &cfg)
+	return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
+	return ctrl.NewControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named("dynamicresourceallocationconfig_controller").
+		For(&kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{}).
+		WithEventFilter(predicate.Funcs{
+			// Only singleton named "default" in "kueue-system" namespace matters.
+			CreateFunc: func(e event.CreateEvent) bool {
+				obj := e.Object.(*kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+				return obj.Name == "default" && obj.Namespace == "kueue-system"
+			},
+			UpdateFunc: func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool {
+				obj := e.ObjectNew.(*kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+				return obj.Name == "default" && obj.Namespace == "kueue-system"
+			},
```

  Why do we need to restrict in this name and namespace?
  IIUC, invalid DRAConfig is rejected by validation.

```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,119 @@
+/*
+Copyright The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at

+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package webhooks
+
+import (
+	"context"
+
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/validation/field"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/webhook"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/webhook/admission"
+
+	kueuev1alpha1 "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/features"
+)
+
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook validates create / update requests.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook struct{}
+
+func setupWebhookForDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
+	return ctrl.NewWebhookManagedBy(mgr).
+		For(&kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{}).
+		WithValidator(&DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook{}).
+		Complete()
+}
+
+// +kubebuilder:webhook:path=/validate-kueue-x-k8s-io-v1alpha1-dynamicresourceallocationconfig,mutating=false,failurePolicy=fail,sideEffects=None,groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=create;update,versions=v1alpha1,name=vdynamicresourceallocationconfig.kb.io,admissionReviewVersions=v1
+
+var _ webhook.CustomValidator = &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook{}
+
+// ValidateCreate blocks CR creation when the feature-gate is off.
+func (w *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook) ValidateCreate(_ context.Context, obj runtime.Object) (admission.Warnings, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return nil, field.Forbidden(field.NewPath(""), "DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is disabled")
+	}
+	draCfg := obj.(*kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+
+	var allErrs field.ErrorList
+	if draCfg.Name != "default" {
+		allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(field.NewPath("metadata", "name"), draCfg.Name, "must be 'default'"))
+	}
+
+	if draCfg.Namespace != "kueue-system" {
+		allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(field.NewPath("metadata", "namespace"), draCfg.Namespace, "must be 'kueue-system'"))
+	}
+
+	if len(allErrs) > 0 {
+		return nil, allErrs.ToAggregate()
+	}
+
+	// structural validation of spec
+	allErrs = append(allErrs, validateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(draCfg)...)
+	if len(allErrs) > 0 {
+		return nil, allErrs.ToAggregate()
+	}
+	return nil, nil
+}
+
+// ValidateUpdate blocks updates when the feature-gate is off.
+func (w *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook) ValidateUpdate(_ context.Context, _ runtime.Object, newObj runtime.Object) (admission.Warnings, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return nil, field.Forbidden(field.NewPath(""), "DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is disabled")
+	}
+	draCfg := newObj.(*kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+	var allErrs field.ErrorList
+
+	if draCfg.Name != "default" {
```

  updated, the only thing in webhook now is the namespace check, which is not available at compile time and it is coming from cfg.Namespace

```diff
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfig is a singleton CRD that maps a logical resource name to one or more DeviceClasses

+	// +kubebuilder:validation:MaxItems=16
+	Resources []DynamicResource `json:"resources"`
+}

+// DynamicResource describes a single logical resource and the DeviceClasses mapping. The resource name is used
+// to quota in ClusterQueue.

+	// Name is referenced in ClusterQueue.nominalQuota and Workload status.
```

```diff
+/*

+package core
+
+import (
+	"context"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/cache"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/features"
+)
+
+// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=get;list;watch
+
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler keeps the cache's DeviceClass→logical-resource
+// mapping in sync with the singleton DynamicResourceAllocationConfig object.
+// It is only registered when the DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is enabled.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	cache  *cache.Cache
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+func NewDRAConfigReconciler(client client.Client, c *cache.Cache) *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler {
+	return &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		cache:  c,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName("dra-config-reconciler"),
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+
+	var cfg kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig
+	if err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &cfg); err != nil {
+		// TODO: this should never happen. But if a user deletes the singleton DRA by mistake, we should
+		//  have a way to gracefully handle it. May be adding a finalizer to the singleton DRAConfig object?
+		return ctrl.Result{}, client.IgnoreNotFound(err)
+	}
+
+	r.log.V(2).Info("Reconciling DynamicResourceAllocationConfig", "name", req.NamespacedName)
+	// we do not expect a lot of reconciles triggered here, therefore directly updating the cache should be okay
+	r.cache.AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(r.log, &cfg)
+	return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
+	return ctrl.NewControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named("dynamicresourceallocationconfig_controller").
+		For(&kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{}).
+		WithEventFilter(predicate.Funcs{
+			// Only singleton named "default" in "kueue-system" namespace matters.
+			CreateFunc: func(e event.CreateEvent) bool {
+				obj := e.Object.(*kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+				return obj.Name == "default" && obj.Namespace == "kueue-system"
+			},
+			UpdateFunc: func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool {
+				obj := e.ObjectNew.(*kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+				return obj.Name == "default" && obj.Namespace == "kueue-system"
+			},
```

  This is just being pedantic about it, it can be removed.  The original reason was, in case the webhook is removed or dysfunctional for some reason, this makes sure that reconciled are not triggered for bogus objects.

### Review by [@alaypatel07](https://github.com/alaypatel07) (commented) — 2025-07-18T18:31:35Z

- **pkg/cache/cache.go:1034** by [@alaypatel07](https://github.com/alaypatel07) — 2025-07-18T18:31:34Z
```diff
@@ -986,3 +989,30 @@ func (c *Cache) MatchingClusterQueues(nsLabels map[string]string) sets.Set[kueue
 func queueKey(q *kueue.LocalQueue) queue.LocalQueueReference {
 	return queue.NewLocalQueueReference(q.Namespace, kueue.LocalQueueName(q.Name))
 }
+
+// AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig ingests the singleton CRD and updates
+// the in-memory DeviceClass → logical resource map.
+// It is idempotent and thread-safe.
+func (c *Cache) AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(log logr.Logger, draCfg *kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig) {
+	c.Lock()
+	defer c.Unlock()
+
+	// Rebuild from scratch to avoid stale entries.
+	newMap := make(map[corev1.ResourceName]corev1.ResourceName)
+	for _, res := range draCfg.Spec.Resources {
+		for _, dc := range res.DeviceClassNames {
+			newMap[dc] = res.Name
+		}
+	}
+	c.draDeviceClassToResource = newMap
+	log.V(2).Info("Updated DRA DeviceClass mapping", "entries", len(newMap))
+}
+
+// GetResourceNameForDeviceClass converts a DeviceClass to its logical resource name.
+// Returns (logicalRes, true) on success or ("", false) when unmapped.
+func (c *Cache) GetResourceNameForDeviceClass(dc corev1.ResourceName) (corev1.ResourceName, bool) {
+	c.RLock()
+	defer c.RUnlock()
+	lr, ok := c.draDeviceClassToResource[dc]
+	return lr, ok
```

  this suggestion wont compile, `return c.draDeviceClassToResource[dc]` will return a single value, the only way to force the lookup to return multiple values is by `lr, ok := c.draDeviceClassToResource[dc]`


  I don't agree with this comment. Admin can create CRDs and/or remove them at will. If we build and publish this CRD at install time then we could assume that this does not happen.
  
  But we should expect cases where this object does not exist and we should handle if its deleted.

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2025-07-22T16:12:36Z

- **pkg/cache/cache.go:1033** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2025-07-22T16:12:36Z
```diff
@@ -986,3 +989,30 @@ func (c *Cache) MatchingClusterQueues(nsLabels map[string]string) sets.Set[kueue
 func queueKey(q *kueue.LocalQueue) queue.LocalQueueReference {
 	return queue.NewLocalQueueReference(q.Namespace, kueue.LocalQueueName(q.Name))
 }
+
+// AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig ingests the singleton CRD and updates
+// the in-memory DeviceClass → logical resource map.
+// It is idempotent and thread-safe.
+func (c *Cache) AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(log logr.Logger, draCfg *kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig) {
+	c.Lock()
+	defer c.Unlock()
+
+	// Rebuild from scratch to avoid stale entries.
+	deviceClassNameToResName := make(map[corev1.ResourceName]corev1.ResourceName)
+	for _, res := range draCfg.Spec.Resources {
+		for _, dc := range res.DeviceClassNames {
+			deviceClassNameToResName[dc] = res.Name
+		}
+	}
+	c.draDeviceClassToResource = deviceClassNameToResName
+	log.V(2).Info("Updated DRA DeviceClass mapping", "entries", len(deviceClassNameToResName))
+}
+
+// GetResourceNameForDeviceClass converts a DeviceClass to its logical resource name.
+// Returns (logicalRes, true) on success or ("", false) when unmapped.
+func (c *Cache) GetResourceNameForDeviceClass(dc corev1.ResourceName) (corev1.ResourceName, bool) {
+	c.RLock()
+	defer c.RUnlock()
+	lr, ok := c.draDeviceClassToResource[dc]
```

  Please gate the code by the feature gate, just 
  
  ```golang
  if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
   return
  }
  ```

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2025-07-22T16:14:29Z

- **pkg/controller/core/dynamicresourceallocationconfig_controller.go:55** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2025-07-22T16:14:29Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,90 @@
+/*
+Copyright The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package core
+
+import (
+	"context"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/cache"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/features"
+)
+
+// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=get;list;watch
+
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler keeps the cache's DeviceClass→logical-resource
+// mapping in sync with the singleton DynamicResourceAllocationConfig object.
+// It is only registered when the DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is enabled.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler struct {
+	client    client.Client
+	cache     *cache.Cache
+	log       logr.Logger
+	namespace string
+}
+
+func NewDRAConfigReconciler(client client.Client, c *cache.Cache, namespace string) *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler {
+	return &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler{
+		client:    client,
+		cache:     c,
+		log:       ctrl.Log.WithName("dra-config-reconciler"),
+		namespace: namespace,
+	}
+}
+

+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
```

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2025-07-22T16:16:45Z

```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,90 @@
+/*

+package core
+
+import (
+	"context"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/cache"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/features"
+)
+
+// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=get;list;watch
+
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler keeps the cache's DeviceClass→logical-resource
+// mapping in sync with the singleton DynamicResourceAllocationConfig object.
+// It is only registered when the DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is enabled.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler struct {
+	client    client.Client
+	cache     *cache.Cache
+	log       logr.Logger
+	namespace string
+}
+
+func NewDRAConfigReconciler(client client.Client, c *cache.Cache, namespace string) *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler {
+	return &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler{
+		client:    client,
+		cache:     c,
+		log:       ctrl.Log.WithName("dra-config-reconciler"),
+		namespace: namespace,
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+
+	var cfg kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig
+	if err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &cfg); err != nil {
+		// TODO: this should never happen. But if a user deletes the singleton DRA by mistake, we should
+		//  have a way to gracefully handle it. May be adding a finalizer to the singleton DRAConfig object?
+		return ctrl.Result{}, client.IgnoreNotFound(err)
+	}
+
+	r.log.V(2).Info("Reconciling DynamicResourceAllocationConfig", "name", req.NamespacedName)
+	// we do not expect a lot of reconciles triggered here, therefore directly updating the cache should be okay
+	r.cache.AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(r.log, &cfg)
+	return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
+	return ctrl.NewControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named("dynamicresourceallocationconfig_controller").
+		For(&kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{}).
+		WithEventFilter(predicate.Funcs{
+			// Only singleton named "default" in the configured namespace matters.
+			CreateFunc: func(e event.CreateEvent) bool {
+				obj := e.Object.(*kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+				return obj.Name == "default" && obj.Namespace == r.namespace
+			},
+			UpdateFunc: func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool {
+				obj := e.ObjectNew.(*kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+				return obj.Name == "default" && obj.Namespace == r.namespace
+			},
```

  No need for the checks. We can ensure this is singleton using CEL, so that inside the codebase we can just rely on that.

```diff
+// Sentinel errors for specific conditions that callers can check with errors.Is()
+var (
+	ErrDeviceClassNotMapped = errors.New("DeviceClass is not mapped in DynamicResourceAllocationConfig")
+	ErrResourceClaimInUse   = errors.New("ResourceClaim is used by another workload")
+	ErrClaimSpecNotFound    = errors.New("failed to get claim spec")
+)
+
+// countDevicesPerClass returns a map[DeviceClass]→Quantity representing the
+// total number of devices requested for each DeviceClass inside the provided
+// ResourceClaimSpec.
+//
+// When structured-parameters are used (beta in k8s 1.32/1.33) **every entry**
+// in `spec.devices.requests` represents one device, so the quantity is the
+// sum of all `exactly` entries that reference the same DeviceClass.
+func countDevicesPerClass(claimSpec *resourcev1beta1.ResourceClaimSpec) map[corev1.ResourceName]resource.Quantity {
+	out := make(map[corev1.ResourceName]resource.Quantity)
+	if claimSpec == nil {
+		return out
+	}
+	for _, req := range claimSpec.Devices.Requests {
+		dc := corev1.ResourceName(req.DeviceClassName)
+		if dc == "" {
+			continue
+		}
+		var q int64
+		if req.AllocationMode == resourcev1beta1.DeviceAllocationModeExactCount {
```

  Is is expected to count 0 when "all" mode is used?

### Review by [@tenzen-y](https://github.com/tenzen-y) (commented) — 2025-07-22T17:07:29Z

- **pkg/cache/cache.go:1034** by [@tenzen-y](https://github.com/tenzen-y) — 2025-07-22T17:07:29Z
```diff
@@ -986,3 +989,30 @@ func (c *Cache) MatchingClusterQueues(nsLabels map[string]string) sets.Set[kueue
 func queueKey(q *kueue.LocalQueue) queue.LocalQueueReference {
 	return queue.NewLocalQueueReference(q.Namespace, kueue.LocalQueueName(q.Name))
 }
+
+// AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig ingests the singleton CRD and updates
+// the in-memory DeviceClass → logical resource map.
+// It is idempotent and thread-safe.
+func (c *Cache) AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(log logr.Logger, draCfg *kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig) {
+	c.Lock()
+	defer c.Unlock()
+
+	// Rebuild from scratch to avoid stale entries.
+	newMap := make(map[corev1.ResourceName]corev1.ResourceName)
+	for _, res := range draCfg.Spec.Resources {
+		for _, dc := range res.DeviceClassNames {
+			newMap[dc] = res.Name
+		}
+	}
+	c.draDeviceClassToResource = newMap
+	log.V(2).Info("Updated DRA DeviceClass mapping", "entries", len(newMap))
+}
+
+// GetResourceNameForDeviceClass converts a DeviceClass to its logical resource name.
+// Returns (logicalRes, true) on success or ("", false) when unmapped.
+func (c *Cache) GetResourceNameForDeviceClass(dc corev1.ResourceName) (corev1.ResourceName, bool) {
+	c.RLock()
+	defer c.RUnlock()
+	lr, ok := c.draDeviceClassToResource[dc]
+	return lr, ok
```

  Oh, that makes sense.
  Thank you for checking that.

### Review by [@alaypatel07](https://github.com/alaypatel07) (commented) — 2025-08-05T22:44:29Z

```diff
+// AddDeviceClassesToContainerRequests augments the workload copy with logical

+// lookup converts DeviceClass → logical resource; caller can pass
+// cache.GetResourceNameForDeviceClass.
+func AddDeviceClassesToContainerRequests(ctx context.Context, cl client.Client, wl *kueue.Workload, cqName string, lookup func(dc corev1.ResourceName) (corev1.ResourceName, bool)) error {
```

  @mimowo I was not super excited about the mutation aspect as well. However, it does make the implementation very easy.
  
  I have modified the PR, check the latest 4 commits, its a step by step implementation of an alternative approach that eliminates workload mutation.
  
  To summarize the alternative approach, the implementation:
  1. calculates DRA resources during workload.Info creation (Kueue's internal abstraction for cache/queue resource calculations) without modifying original workload objects
  2. initializes DRA support in queue manager to preserve the resources through scheduling/admission
  3. ensures DRA resources appear in the workload admission status for proper quota tracking and visibility.
  
  Since the alternative approach was not discussed during design, I am using a very rough POC implementation without tests to continue this discussion, I will add relevant unit tests if we prefer to implement it.
  
  I have also ran the manual test against it, it is passing, so the implementation works.
  
  cc @kannon92 @tenzen-y

```diff
+
+// AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig ingests the singleton CRD and updates
+// the in-memory DeviceClass → logical resource map.
+// It is idempotent and thread-safe.
+func (c *Cache) AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(log logr.Logger, draCfg *kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig) {
+	c.Lock()
+	defer c.Unlock()
+
+	// Rebuild from scratch to avoid stale entries.
+	deviceClassNameToResName := make(map[corev1.ResourceName]corev1.ResourceName)
+	for _, res := range draCfg.Spec.Resources {
+		for _, dc := range res.DeviceClassNames {
+			deviceClassNameToResName[dc] = res.Name
+		}
+	}
+	c.draDeviceClassToResource = deviceClassNameToResName
+	log.V(2).Info("Updated DRA DeviceClass mapping", "entries", len(deviceClassNameToResName))
+}
+
+// GetResourceNameForDeviceClass converts a DeviceClass to its logical resource name.
+// Returns (logicalRes, true) on success or ("", false) when unmapped.
+func (c *Cache) GetResourceNameForDeviceClass(dc corev1.ResourceName) (corev1.ResourceName, bool) {
+	c.RLock()
+	defer c.RUnlock()
+	lr, ok := c.draDeviceClassToResource[dc]
```

  same as here: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/5873/files#r2264932135

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2025-08-11T17:24:14Z

```diff
@@ -433,7 +439,11 @@ func (c *clusterQueue) addOrUpdateWorkload(log logr.Logger, w *kueue.Workload) {
 	if _, exist := c.Workloads[k]; exist {

-	wi := workload.NewInfo(w, c.workloadInfoOptions...)
+	// Build InfoOptions with DRA config when enabled. We don't handle DRA errors here:
```

  Instead please follow this pattern:
  ```golang
  infoOptions := slices.Copy(c.workloadInfoOptions)
  if features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
    infoOptions = append(infoOptions, workload.BuildDRAWorkloadInfoOptions(c.draClient, string(c.Name), c.draLookup))
  }
  wi := workload.NewInfo(w, infoOptions...)
  ```
  Then it is clear for the reader the new code is separated out

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2025-08-11T18:09:03Z

  Readability: this function name `BuildDRAWorkloadInfoOptions` clearly suggests it should only return DRA options, but it has more responsibilities now. Maybe if we renamed like `AppendDRAWorkloadOptions` it would be better. Still, I like the single-responsibility principle - just return the DRA-specific options.
  
  > Readability wise, are you recommending to transfer the feature gate check from inside the function to outside?
  
  Yes, but I'm ok even with the "defensive" checks being done at two layers, they only take nanoseconds probably, but help us to make sure the new code is isolated.

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2025-08-11T18:27:04Z

- **pkg/workload/workload.go:522** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2025-08-11T18:27:04Z
```diff
@@ -479,7 +510,46 @@ func totalRequestsFromPodSets(wl *kueue.Workload, info *InfoOptions) []PodSetRes
 		setRes.Requests.Mul(int64(count))
 		res = append(res, setRes)
 	}
-	return res
+
+	if features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) && info.dra != nil && info.dra.enabled {
+		psRCTReq, err := dra.GetResourceRequestsForResourceClaimTemplates(context.Background(), info.dra.client, wl, info.dra.lookup)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get resource requests for resource claim templates: %w", err)
+		}
+		psRCReq, err := dra.GetResourceRequestsForResourceClaims(context.Background(), info.dra.client, wl, info.dra.clusterQueue, info.dra.lookup)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get resource requests for resource claims: %w", err)
+		}
```

  We should avoid calling `context.Background()` , but the external context.
  
  For example, when Kueue is shutting down (context cancelled) we don't want these zombie goroutines to continue. Another reason is that the context carries useful information for logging, and using background we cut off that information.
  
  Actually, I analyzed the code, and I think (unless missed something) it will be better to read the mapping and pump though the InfoOptions the entire mapping. Then, we can fetch and read / parse the mapping in places where we have the context and error handling. 
  
  Another alternative is to propagate the context via NewInfo, and make the NewInfo return errors, but this seems more involving.

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2025-08-11T18:55:03Z

- **pkg/workload/workload.go:522** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2025-08-11T18:55:03Z
```diff
@@ -479,7 +510,46 @@ func totalRequestsFromPodSets(wl *kueue.Workload, info *InfoOptions) []PodSetRes
 		setRes.Requests.Mul(int64(count))
 		res = append(res, setRes)
 	}
-	return res
+
+	if features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) && info.dra != nil && info.dra.enabled {
+		psRCTReq, err := dra.GetResourceRequestsForResourceClaimTemplates(context.Background(), info.dra.client, wl, info.dra.lookup)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get resource requests for resource claim templates: %w", err)
+		}
+		psRCReq, err := dra.GetResourceRequestsForResourceClaims(context.Background(), info.dra.client, wl, info.dra.clusterQueue, info.dra.lookup)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get resource requests for resource claims: %w", err)
+		}
```

  OH, I think I understand - we pass the lookup function, because the mapping could change in the lifetime if the system, without restart.  This is a substantial change into Kueue. 
  
  I would suggest to start simple: require Kueue restart whenever the mapping is changed, this would be inlined in our philosophy so far. 
  
  I understand it is valuable to make the mapping reload as the CRD is changed, but I would call it a separate enhancement PR, for the ease of reviewing, and to make sure we have a test for it. Otherwise the PR feels overwhelming currently.
  
  Then, as suggested in the previous comment in the alternative I think it will be better to propagate the context, and the error via the NewInfo.

```diff
+import (

+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook validates create / update requests.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook struct {
+	namespace string
+}
+
+func setupWebhookForDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(mgr ctrl.Manager, namespace string) error {
+	return ctrl.NewWebhookManagedBy(mgr).
+		For(&kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{}).
+		WithValidator(&DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook{namespace: namespace}).
+		Complete()
+}
+
+// +kubebuilder:webhook:path=/validate-kueue-x-k8s-io-v1alpha1-dynamicresourceallocationconfig,mutating=false,failurePolicy=fail,sideEffects=None,groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=create;update,versions=v1alpha1,name=vdynamicresourceallocationconfig.kb.io,admissionReviewVersions=v1
+
+var _ webhook.CustomValidator = &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook{}
+
+// ValidateCreate blocks CR creation when the feature-gate is off.
+func (w *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook) ValidateCreate(_ context.Context, obj runtime.Object) (admission.Warnings, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
```

  I'm not sure it is a blocker, but it seems we still have enough time for 0.14 to aim for the desired state. 
  
  I think using CEL is better than webhooks (performance and readability). 
  
  If we are time-constrained, and some validation is hard to express in CEL, then I would rather not add the validation in the first iteration, but only add in a follow up, rather than leaving webhook -> CEL rewrite as a follow up. It is always hard, from my experience, to proceed with rewrite.

### Review by [@kannon92](https://github.com/kannon92) (commented) — 2025-08-11T19:54:55Z

- **pkg/webhooks/dynamicresourceallocationconfig_webhook.go:101** by [@kannon92](https://github.com/kannon92) — 2025-08-11T19:54:55Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,112 @@
+/*
+Copyright The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package webhooks
+
+import (
+	"context"
+
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/validation/field"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/webhook"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/webhook/admission"
+
+	kueuev1alpha1 "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/features"
+)
+
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook validates create / update requests.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook struct{}
+
+func setupWebhookForDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
+	return ctrl.NewWebhookManagedBy(mgr).
+		For(&kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{}).
+		WithValidator(&DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook{}).
+		Complete()
+}
+
+// +kubebuilder:webhook:path=/validate-kueue-x-k8s-io-v1alpha1-dynamicresourceallocationconfig,mutating=false,failurePolicy=fail,sideEffects=None,groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=create;update,versions=v1alpha1,name=vdynamicresourceallocationconfig.kb.io,admissionReviewVersions=v1
+
+var _ webhook.CustomValidator = &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook{}
+
+// ValidateCreate blocks CR creation when the feature-gate is off.
+func (w *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook) ValidateCreate(_ context.Context, obj runtime.Object) (admission.Warnings, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return nil, field.Forbidden(field.NewPath(""), "DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is disabled")
+	}
+	draCfg := obj.(*kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+
+	var allErrs field.ErrorList
+	if draCfg.Name != "default" {
+		allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(field.NewPath("metadata", "name"), draCfg.Name, "must be 'default'"))
+	}
+	if draCfg.Namespace != "" {
+		allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(field.NewPath("metadata", "namespace"), draCfg.Namespace, "must be empty for cluster-scoped resource"))
+	}
+
+	allErrs = append(allErrs, validateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(draCfg)...)
+
+	if len(allErrs) > 0 {
+		return nil, allErrs.ToAggregate()
+	}
+	return nil, nil
+}
+
+// ValidateUpdate blocks updates when the feature-gate is off.
+func (w *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook) ValidateUpdate(_ context.Context, _ runtime.Object, newObj runtime.Object) (admission.Warnings, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return nil, field.Forbidden(field.NewPath(""), "DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is disabled")
+	}
+	draCfg := newObj.(*kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+	var allErrs field.ErrorList
+
+	if draCfg.Name != "default" {
+		allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(field.NewPath("metadata", "name"), draCfg.Name, "must be 'default'"))
+	}
+	if draCfg.Namespace != "" {
+		allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(field.NewPath("metadata", "namespace"), draCfg.Namespace, "must be empty for cluster-scoped resource"))
+	}
+
+	allErrs = append(allErrs, validateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(draCfg)...)
+
+	if len(allErrs) > 0 {
+		return nil, allErrs.ToAggregate()
+	}
+
+	return nil, nil
+}
+
+// ValidateDelete – no special handling.
+func (w *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook) ValidateDelete(_ context.Context, _ runtime.Object) (admission.Warnings, error) {
+	return nil, nil
+}
+
+func validateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(draCfg *kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig) field.ErrorList {
+	var allErrs field.ErrorList
+
+	for i := range draCfg.Spec.Resources {
```

  I think you need to enforce uniqueness in these lists.
  
  I don't think `listMapType` actually does that for you.

  Do we need this? Why not just rely on the feature gate?
  
  IIUC we could check DRA feature enablement based on the gate. If the DRA mapping is not supplied then we just have `preprocessedResources` empty.

```diff
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfig is a singleton CRD that maps a logical resource name to one or more DeviceClasses
```

```diff
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfig struct {

+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`

+	// Resources lists logical resources that Kueue will account.
+	// +listType=map
+	// +listMapKey=name
+	// +kubebuilder:validation:MinItems=1
+	// +kubebuilder:validation:MaxItems=16
+	Resources []DynamicResource `json:"resources"`
+}
+
+// DynamicResource describes a single logical resource and the DeviceClasses mapping. The resource name is used
+// to quota in ClusterQueue.
+type DynamicResource struct {
+	// Name is referenced in ClusterQueue.nominalQuota and Workload status.
```

  you can resolve this.

### Review by [@kannon92](https://github.com/kannon92) (commented) — 2025-08-21T01:38:38Z

- **apis/kueue/v1alpha1/dynamicresourceallocationconfig_types.go:17** by [@kannon92](https://github.com/kannon92) — 2025-08-21T01:38:38Z

  @tenzen-y @gabesaba  
  
  We are really interested in the DRA integration for Openshfit Kueue. But we also tend to discourage the use of alpha APIs for our users.
  
  Is there any room to start this API in beta? 
  
  The API doesn't seem too complicated and DRA is GA in 1.34 so imo it looks a bit odd that DRA is alpha for something that is GA in upstream.
  
  Right now, we would have to discourage kueue users to use DRA until this work is further along. I would love for you all to consider starting the dynamicconfigurationallocationconfig as a v1beta1 API with the other core components.
  
  I am fine with the feature being alpha but curious if the API has to start as alpha.

### Review by [@tenzen-y](https://github.com/tenzen-y) (commented) — 2025-08-21T01:53:02Z

- **apis/kueue/v1alpha1/dynamicresourceallocationconfig_types.go:17** by [@tenzen-y](https://github.com/tenzen-y) — 2025-08-21T01:53:01Z
```diff
@@ -17,15 +17,19 @@ limitations under the License.
 package v1alpha1
```

  We should have Alpha in the first release to have the ability to break APIs based on feedback and combinations of other new features (not only for DRA). 
  
  Kueue DRAConfig API is not part of DRA feature. That is connection to meet Kueue and DRA, then alpha is still reasonable.
  
  Starting from Alpha based on downstream support matrix (Openshift is downstream) means downstream enforce the API maintainance costs to upstream since we can not break Beta API w/o conversion webhook.
  
  Upstream should be first.

```diff
+
+package webhooks
+
+import (
+	"context"
+
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/validation/field"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/webhook"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/webhook/admission"
+
+	kueuev1alpha1 "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/features"
+)
+
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook validates create / update requests.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook struct{}
+
+func setupWebhookForDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
+	return ctrl.NewWebhookManagedBy(mgr).
+		For(&kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{}).
+		WithValidator(&DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook{}).
+		Complete()
+}
+
+// +kubebuilder:webhook:path=/validate-kueue-x-k8s-io-v1alpha1-dynamicresourceallocationconfig,mutating=false,failurePolicy=fail,sideEffects=None,groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=create;update,versions=v1alpha1,name=vdynamicresourceallocationconfig.kb.io,admissionReviewVersions=v1
+
+var _ webhook.CustomValidator = &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook{}
+
+// ValidateCreate blocks CR creation when the feature-gate is off.
+func (w *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook) ValidateCreate(_ context.Context, obj runtime.Object) (admission.Warnings, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return nil, field.Forbidden(field.NewPath(""), "DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is disabled")
+	}
+	draCfg := obj.(*kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+
+	var allErrs field.ErrorList
+	if draCfg.Name != "default" {
+		allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(field.NewPath("metadata", "name"), draCfg.Name, "must be 'default'"))
+	}
+	if draCfg.Namespace != "" {
+		allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(field.NewPath("metadata", "namespace"), draCfg.Namespace, "must be empty for cluster-scoped resource"))
+	}
+
+	allErrs = append(allErrs, validateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(draCfg)...)
+
+	if len(allErrs) > 0 {
+		return nil, allErrs.ToAggregate()
+	}
+	return nil, nil
+}
+
+// ValidateUpdate blocks updates when the feature-gate is off.
+func (w *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook) ValidateUpdate(_ context.Context, _ runtime.Object, newObj runtime.Object) (admission.Warnings, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return nil, field.Forbidden(field.NewPath(""), "DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is disabled")
+	}
+	draCfg := newObj.(*kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+	var allErrs field.ErrorList
+
+	if draCfg.Name != "default" {
+		allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(field.NewPath("metadata", "name"), draCfg.Name, "must be 'default'"))
+	}
+	if draCfg.Namespace != "" {
+		allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(field.NewPath("metadata", "namespace"), draCfg.Namespace, "must be empty for cluster-scoped resource"))
+	}
+
+	allErrs = append(allErrs, validateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(draCfg)...)
+
+	if len(allErrs) > 0 {
+		return nil, allErrs.ToAggregate()
+	}
+
+	return nil, nil
+}
+
+// ValidateDelete – no special handling.
+func (w *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigWebhook) ValidateDelete(_ context.Context, _ runtime.Object) (admission.Warnings, error) {
+	return nil, nil
+}
+
+func validateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(draCfg *kueuev1alpha1.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig) field.ErrorList {
+	var allErrs field.ErrorList
+
+	for i := range draCfg.Spec.Resources {
```

  ```
    DEBUG DUPLICATE: Expected error received: DynamicResourceAllocationConfig.kueue.x-k8s.io "default" is invalid: spec.resources[1]: Duplicate value: map[string]interface {}{"name":"gpus"}
    ```
    
    the listMapType indeed blocks duplicate entry, this was discussed during KEP process.
    
    I have added an integration test to verify this.

```diff
+
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler keeps the cache's DeviceClass→logical-resource
+// mapping in sync with the singleton DynamicResourceAllocationConfig object.
+// It is only registered when the DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is enabled.

+	client    client.Client
+	cache     *cache.Cache
+	log       logr.Logger
+	namespace string
+}
+
+func NewDRAConfigReconciler(client client.Client, c *cache.Cache, namespace string) *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler {
+	return &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler{
+		client:    client,
+		cache:     c,
+		log:       ctrl.Log.WithName("dra-config-reconciler"),
+		namespace: namespace,
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+
+	var cfg kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig
+	if err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &cfg); err != nil {
+		// TODO: this should never happen. But if a user deletes the singleton DRA by mistake, we should
```

  We use finalizers for CQ and RF.
  
  If a workload or CQ is using a RF, we set a finalizer.

```diff
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"

+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/cache"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/features"

+// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=get;list;watch
```

```diff
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler keeps the cache's DeviceClass→logical-resource
+// mapping in sync with the singleton DynamicResourceAllocationConfig object.
+// It is only registered when the DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is enabled.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler struct {
+	client    client.Client
+	cache     *cache.Cache
+	log       logr.Logger
+	namespace string
+}
+
+func NewDRAConfigReconciler(client client.Client, c *cache.Cache, namespace string) *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler {
+	return &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler{
+		client:    client,
+		cache:     c,
+		log:       ctrl.Log.WithName("dra-config-reconciler"),
+		namespace: namespace,
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+
+	var cfg kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig
+	if err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &cfg); err != nil {
+		// TODO: this should never happen. But if a user deletes the singleton DRA by mistake, we should
```

  I'm also okay to file this as issue for a future work.
  
  But what would be the behavior if someone deletes this and the CQ references it?

### Review by [@rphillips](https://github.com/rphillips) (commented) — 2025-08-22T22:23:40Z

- **pkg/dra/claims.go:175** by [@rphillips](https://github.com/rphillips) — 2025-08-22T22:23:40Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,195 @@
+/*
+Copyright The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package dra
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"errors"
+	"fmt"
+	"strconv"
+
+	corev1 "k8s.io/api/core/v1"
+	resourcev1beta2 "k8s.io/api/resource/v1beta2"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/resource"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1beta1"
+	utilresource "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/resource"
+)
+
+var (
+	ErrDeviceClassNotMapped = errors.New("DeviceClass is not mapped in DynamicResourceAllocationConfig")
+	ErrResourceClaimInUse   = errors.New("ResourceClaim is used by another workload")
+	ErrClaimSpecNotFound    = errors.New("failed to get claim spec")
+)
+
+// countDevicesPerClass returns a map[DeviceClass]->Quantity representing the
+// total number of devices requested for each DeviceClass inside the provided
+// ResourceClaimSpec.
+func countDevicesPerClass(claimSpec *resourcev1beta2.ResourceClaimSpec) map[corev1.ResourceName]resource.Quantity {
+	out := make(map[corev1.ResourceName]resource.Quantity)
+	if claimSpec == nil {
+		return out
+	}
+	for _, req := range claimSpec.Devices.Requests {
+		// v1beta2 DeviceRequest has Exactly or FirstAvailable. For Step 1, we
+		// preserve existing semantics by only supporting Exactly with Count.
+		var dcName string
+		var q int64
+		if req.Exactly != nil {
+			dcName = req.Exactly.DeviceClassName
+			if req.Exactly.AllocationMode == resourcev1beta2.DeviceAllocationModeExactCount {
+				q = req.Exactly.Count
+			}
+		}
+		dc := corev1.ResourceName(dcName)
+		if dc == "" {
+			continue
+		}
+		// TODO: handle other Allocation modes
+		if existing, found := out[dc]; found {
+			existing.Add(resource.MustParse(strconv.FormatInt(q, 10)))
+			out[dc] = existing
+		} else {
+			out[dc] = resource.MustParse(strconv.FormatInt(q, 10))
+		}
+	}
+	return out
+}
+
+// getClaimSpec resolves the ResourceClaim(Template) referenced by the PodResourceClaim
+// and returns its *ResourceClaimSpec. A nil spec and nil error mean the reference is
+// empty (both name pointers are nil) and should be skipped.
+func getClaimSpec(ctx context.Context, cl client.Client, namespace string, prc corev1.PodResourceClaim) (*resourcev1beta2.ResourceClaimSpec, error) {
+	switch {
+	case prc.ResourceClaimTemplateName != nil:
+		var tmpl resourcev1beta2.ResourceClaimTemplate
+		if err := cl.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKey{Namespace: namespace, Name: *prc.ResourceClaimTemplateName}, &tmpl); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+		return &tmpl.Spec.Spec, nil
+	case prc.ResourceClaimName != nil:
+		var claim resourcev1beta2.ResourceClaim
+		if err := cl.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKey{Namespace: namespace, Name: *prc.ResourceClaimName}, &claim); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+		return &claim.Spec, nil
+	default:
+		return nil, nil
+	}
+}
+
+// GetResourceRequestsForResourceClaimTemplates walks all ResourceClaimTemplates referenced by each PodSet of the Workload,
+// converts DeviceClass counts into logical resources using the provided lookup function and
+// returns the aggregated quantities per PodSet.
+//
+// If at least one DeviceClass is not present in the DynamicResourceAllocationConfig the function
+// returns an error.
+func GetResourceRequestsForResourceClaimTemplates(
+	ctx context.Context,
+	cl client.Client,
+	wl *kueue.Workload,
+	lookup func(dc corev1.ResourceName) (corev1.ResourceName, bool),
+) (map[kueue.PodSetReference]corev1.ResourceList, error) {
+	perPodSet := make(map[kueue.PodSetReference]corev1.ResourceList)
+	for i := range wl.Spec.PodSets {
+		ps := &wl.Spec.PodSets[i]
+		aggregated := corev1.ResourceList{}
+
+		// Resolve every ResourceClaim reference in the PodSet template.
+		for _, prc := range ps.Template.Spec.ResourceClaims {
+			if prc.ResourceClaimTemplateName == nil {
+				continue
+			}
+			spec, err := getClaimSpec(ctx, cl, wl.Namespace, prc)
+			if err != nil {
+				return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get claim spec for ResourceClaimTemplate %s in workload %s podset %s: %w", *prc.ResourceClaimTemplateName, wl.Name, ps.Name, fmt.Errorf("%w: %v", ErrClaimSpecNotFound, err))
+			}
+			if spec == nil {
+				continue
+			}
+
+			for dc, qty := range countDevicesPerClass(spec) {
+				logical, found := lookup(dc)
+				if !found {
+					return nil, fmt.Errorf("DeviceClass %s is not mapped in DynamicResourceAllocationConfig for workload %s podset %s: %w", dc, wl.Name, ps.Name, ErrDeviceClassNotMapped)
+				}
+				aggregated = utilresource.MergeResourceListKeepSum(aggregated, corev1.ResourceList{logical: qty})
+			}
+		}
+
+		if len(aggregated) > 0 {
+			perPodSet[ps.Name] = aggregated
+		}
+	}
+
+	return perPodSet, nil
+}
+
+// GetResourceRequestsForResourceClaims walks all ResourceClaims referenced by each PodSet of the Workload,
+// converts DeviceClass counts into logical resources using the provided lookup function and
+// returns the aggregated quantities per PodSet.
+//
+// If at least one DeviceClass is not present in the DynamicResourceAllocationConfig the function
+// returns an error.
+func GetResourceRequestsForResourceClaims(ctx context.Context,
+	cl client.Client,
+	wl *kueue.Workload,
+	cqName string,
+	lookup func(dc corev1.ResourceName) (corev1.ResourceName, bool)) (map[kueue.PodSetReference]corev1.ResourceList, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+
+	perPodSet := make(map[kueue.PodSetReference]corev1.ResourceList)
+	for i := range wl.Spec.PodSets {
+		ps := &wl.Spec.PodSets[i]
+		aggregated := corev1.ResourceList{}
+
+		for _, prc := range ps.Template.Spec.ResourceClaims {
+			if prc.ResourceClaimName == nil {
+				continue
+			}
+			spec, err := getClaimSpec(ctx, cl, wl.Namespace, prc)
+			if err != nil {
+				return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get claim spec for ResourceClaim %s/%s in workload %s podset %s: %w", wl.Namespace, *prc.ResourceClaimName, wl.Name, ps.Name, fmt.Errorf("%w: %v", ErrClaimSpecNotFound, err))
+			}
+			if spec == nil {
+				continue
+			}
+			claimKey := ClaimKey(fmt.Sprintf("%s/%s", wl.Namespace, *prc.ResourceClaimName))
+
+			allowed := claims.addAndCheckWorkLoad(claimKey, wl.Name)
```

  addAndCheckWorkLoad adds a key to the global claims map. I never see a removal, thus perhaps leading to a memory leak. Did I miss the deletion in claimRefTracker within this PR?

  > Okay. So for Kueue any new CRD must go v1alpha1, v1beta1 and eventually go to v1?
  
  Mostly correct.
  We will have v1beta2 if v1beta1 -> v1 has a breaking change.
  
  > v1 would be once Kueue itself supports v1?
  
  We do not have any decisions. The v1 indicates just the API version, which is separate from the project version.
  Please see https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue?tab=readme-ov-file#production-readiness-status
  
  > ✔️ API version: v1beta1, respecting [Kubernetes Deprecation Policy](https://kubernetes.io/docs/reference/using-api/deprecation-policy/)

- **pkg/controller/core/dynamicresourceallocationconfig_controller.go:73** by [@tenzen-y](https://github.com/tenzen-y) — 2025-08-29T21:06:39Z

```diff
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/dra"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/features"
+)
+
+// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=get;list;watch
+
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler keeps the global DRA mapper's DeviceClass->logical-resource
+// mapping in sync with the singleton DynamicResourceAllocationConfig object.
+// It is only registered when the DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is enabled.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+func NewDRAConfigReconciler(client client.Client) *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler {
+	return &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName("dra-config-reconciler"),
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+
+	var cfg kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig
+	if err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &cfg); err != nil {
+		// TODO: this should never happen. But if a user deletes the singleton DRA by mistake, we should
+		//  have a way to gracefully handle it. May be adding a finalizer to the singleton DRAConfig object?
+		return ctrl.Result{}, client.IgnoreNotFound(err)
+	}
+
+	r.log.V(2).Info("Reconciling DynamicResourceAllocationConfig", "name", req.NamespacedName)
+
+	// Update the global DRA mapper
+	if err := dra.UpdateMapperFromConfig(ctx, &cfg); err != nil {
+		r.log.Error(err, "Failed to update global DRA mapper", "config", req.NamespacedName)
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
```

  ```suggestion
  func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) error {
  ```

```diff
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/features"
+)
+
+// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=get;list;watch
+
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler keeps the global DRA mapper's DeviceClass->logical-resource
+// mapping in sync with the singleton DynamicResourceAllocationConfig object.
+// It is only registered when the DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is enabled.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+func NewDRAConfigReconciler(client client.Client) *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler {
+	return &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName("dra-config-reconciler"),
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+
+	var cfg kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig
+	if err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &cfg); err != nil {
+		// TODO: this should never happen. But if a user deletes the singleton DRA by mistake, we should
+		//  have a way to gracefully handle it. May be adding a finalizer to the singleton DRAConfig object?
+		return ctrl.Result{}, client.IgnoreNotFound(err)
+	}
+
+	r.log.V(2).Info("Reconciling DynamicResourceAllocationConfig", "name", req.NamespacedName)
+
+	// Update the global DRA mapper
+	if err := dra.UpdateMapperFromConfig(ctx, &cfg); err != nil {
+		r.log.Error(err, "Failed to update global DRA mapper", "config", req.NamespacedName)
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
+	return ctrl.NewControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named("dynamicresourceallocationconfig_controller").
+		For(&kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{}).
+		WithEventFilter(predicate.Funcs{
+			// Only singleton named "default" matters (cluster-scoped resource).
+			CreateFunc: func(e event.CreateEvent) bool {
+				obj := e.Object.(*kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+				return obj.Name == "default"
+			},
+			UpdateFunc: func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool {
+				obj := e.ObjectNew.(*kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+				return obj.Name == "default"
+			},
+			DeleteFunc:  func(event.DeleteEvent) bool { return false },
+			GenericFunc: func(event.GenericEvent) bool { return false },
+		}).
+		Complete(r)
```

  ```suggestion
  		Complete(WithLeadingManager(mgr, r, &kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{}, cfg))
  ```

```diff
+package core
```

```diff
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/cache"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/features"
+)
+
+// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=dynamicresourceallocationconfigs,verbs=get;list;watch
+
+// DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler keeps the cache's DeviceClass→logical-resource
+// mapping in sync with the singleton DynamicResourceAllocationConfig object.
+// It is only registered when the DynamicResourceAllocation feature gate is enabled.
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	cache  *cache.Cache
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+func NewDRAConfigReconciler(client client.Client, c *cache.Cache) *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler {
+	return &DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		cache:  c,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName("dra-config-reconciler"),
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+
+	var cfg kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig
+	if err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &cfg); err != nil {
+		// TODO: this should never happen. But if a user deletes the singleton DRA by mistake, we should
+		//  have a way to gracefully handle it. May be adding a finalizer to the singleton DRAConfig object?
+		return ctrl.Result{}, client.IgnoreNotFound(err)
+	}
+
+	r.log.V(2).Info("Reconciling DynamicResourceAllocationConfig", "name", req.NamespacedName)
+	// we do not expect a lot of reconciles triggered here, therefore directly updating the cache should be okay
+	r.cache.AddOrUpdateDynamicResourceAllocationConfig(r.log, &cfg)
+	return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+}
+
+func (r *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
+	return ctrl.NewControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named("dynamicresourceallocationconfig_controller").
+		For(&kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig{}).
+		WithEventFilter(predicate.Funcs{
+			// Only singleton named "default" in "kueue-system" namespace matters.
+			CreateFunc: func(e event.CreateEvent) bool {
+				obj := e.Object.(*kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+				return obj.Name == "default" && obj.Namespace == "kueue-system"
+			},
+			UpdateFunc: func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool {
+				obj := e.ObjectNew.(*kueuealpha.DynamicResourceAllocationConfig)
+				return obj.Name == "default" && obj.Namespace == "kueue-system"
+			},
```

  We can validate the resource name and namespace in the CEL validation, and I think we can avoid such duplicate validations.

```diff
+type DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+func NewDRAConfigReconciler(client client.Client) *DynamicResourceAllocationConfigReconciler {

+		client: client,

+}
+
```
